--- 帖子 #1 ---
This thread will be about my EA Flexy Grid.

It's called Flexy because I want it to be Flexible, I can place the buy/sell grid manually or automatically.
Personally I use it manually because I like to have control. I'm smarter than this EA, the EA doesn't take account of other variable i.e. News and what I'm seeing over my eyes and head.

Manual Flexy Grid
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

Automatic Flexy Grid. When you click the Manual button and it becomes Automatic button in green color, you should see a screenshot like that below. In order to start the EA to trade automatically, you have to click the "START" button. It will become green when you click it. Basically the start button is a safety trigger.
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

The green window on the top right corner contains information regarding the equity, signal etc. I think it's self explanatory, if you don't understand you can ask me.

Anyhow below are the 3 information that might need some explanation while the rest info are self explanatory.
Trading With Line is for Manual trading, it will execute a trade whenever the price crosses the Horizontal line object. In order to place a trade using this method, you have to edit the object name by adding _B or _S.

_B is for buy grid, _S is for sell grid.

Example Buy Grid

Horizontal Line 3951_B

Sell Grid

Horizontal Line 3951_S

Grid Space is the distance between each order. By default it is set to 5 pips space.

Grid is the number of order in a grid. It is depend on the ability the broker's MT4 able to place order. Some broker is able to place 100 orders, some 20, some 50 etc. You can find out by testing it on a demo account or ask their support about the maximum order their MT4 can take.

Example:

If the broker allows you to place 100 Orders, then you should set the grid value to 49 or 50 grid. It will place 49 or 50 trade of Sell/Buy stop and Buy/Sell limit, total 100 order.

I highly suggest you to try this on a demo first. Play around with it first and please give me some of your feedback. I appreciate it.

USER GUIDE (Compiled by OkSHOP)
FLEXY GRID_1.8 (14 - 7 - 2017)

as at 15/7
AUTOMATED
SET A

Alligator - default

ZigZag, 5, 5, 3

RSI, 14

2 EMA (5 and 10) no shift
MANUAL

TRADING WITH LINES INFO:

NAME_1S

or

NAME_1B

1 indicates Grid Style 101

2 indicates Grid Style 111

2 indicates Grid Style 110

B indicates BUY Grid

S indicates SELL Grid.
GRID STYLE (101 / 111 / 110)
Grid style 101, EG BUY GRID VISE VERSA FOR SELL

Sell Stop

Buy

Sell Limit

Buy is the center of the grid

Sell Stop and Sell Limit are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.

So the BUY is meant to be a losing position that got hedged by the Sell orders.
Grid Style 111 EG BUY GRID VISE VERSA FOR SELL

Buy Stop

Buy

Buy Limit

Buy is the center of the grid

Buy Stop and Buy Limit are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.
GRID STYLE 110 BUY VISE VERSA FOR SELL

Buy Stop

Buy

Sell Stop

Buy is the center of the grid

Buy Stop and Sell Stop are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.
PIPS SETTING

5.0 = 5 pip for both (4 & 5 decimal account)

HORIZONTAL LINE

NAME_TP

NAME_SL

NAME_C

TP = It will take profit (close the grid) when there's profit in the grid

SL = It will stop loss (close the grid) when the grid position is losing

C = It will close the grid
BREAKEVEN FUNCTION
1. Grid opened
2. You clicked the breakeven button to green
3. The grid only has 1 opened position at start
4. Further down the line the market executed some of your pending orders.
5. When you have >=2 order gets executed + breakeven button is green = BREAKEVEN function starts working.
You will also be able to set the breakeven function will be run there are >=X active orders.
SO there will be 3 parameters
Parameter 1) Use Breakeven? (Boolean)
Parameter 2) Breakeven amount (double amount $$$)
Parameter 3) Breakeven triggered after X opened orders (integer)

#Post 1 update

Trading With Line is for Manual trading, it will execute a trade whenever the price crosses the Horizontal line object. In order to place a trade using this method, you have to edit the object name by adding _B or _S. In order to enable this feature, you have to make sure the "Use Lines" button is green, you can click it to switch back and forth (Red/green)

_B is for buy grid, _S is for sell grid.

Example Buy Grid

Horizontal Line 3951_B

Sell Grid

Horizontal Line 3951_S

--- 帖子 #6 ---
Thanks for the reply mate. I appreciate it!

GridTradeManually - If it sets to true, means that you will trade manually. It can be override when you click the AUTOMATIC button in the chart.

StartAutomaticTrading - is the safety trigger. When you set gridTradeManually to false and startAutomaticTrading to true, it will trade automatically when you click the Ok button.

ExecuteTradeUsingTrendOrHorizontalLine - It will execute a trade when using the price crosses the Horizontal line. It is use when you trade manually.

backTestMode - is set to true when you want to backtest the automation feature of the EA.

Lots - Is the number of lot per position/order

GridSpace - The grid pips space between each order

maxGrid - Number of stop/limit order. If you set to 20, that mean you will have 20 stop orders and 20 limit orders

TakeProfit - Grid will be close when the profit reaches the take profit amount in term of currency

TradePerDay - This is for automatic grid trading feature. If it set to >1, then per day it will trade as much >1 closed grid. If it set to 0, it will open a grid trade unlimited per day.

startHour - For automatic, at what time do you want the EA to start trigger the trade

endHour - For automatic, at what time do you want the EA to end the grid trading.

stopTradingAfter - For automatic, it will stop trading after it opens several grid trading.

Let say you set it to 5. It will stop trading after the EA closes the 5th grid regardless how many days it takes per grid.

--- 帖子 #12 ---
Thanks for the question and using the EA!

Personally I like to use as maximum maxGrid as I can and as tight GridSpace as the broker can.

So it depends on the broker.

If the broker allows you to place 1000 orders, then i'd love to place total of 1000 orders in a grid.

It is best to use this EA on a single pair. Try not to use it on multiple pair because there could be issue with order placement. For instance when the order has been used on one pair. And the other pair wanted to place a grid order, it will have difficulty because there's no space left to place an order. I hope you can understand what I mean.

For the gridSpace, I usually set to 5 pips.

If I set lower than that, usually there's order issue in the center of the grid because the first stop/limit order is too close to the current price. You can try see it for your self on your demo account and set the EA to manual trading. You will see a missing limit/stop order when you set the gridSpace too low/small.

--- 帖子 #25 ---
Thanks for the feedback mate.

Yes you're right. I cross checked all my close order method, and now only one method that got wrong closeTrades(). :Facepalm:

Inserted Code void tradePositionManager(double profitTarget){
int total;
double winningLossingTrade = buySellProfit(1)+buySellProfit(-1);
if(winningLossingTrade>profitTarget){
total = OrdersTotal();
for(int i=total-1;i>=0;i--)
{
OrderSelect(i, SELECT_BY_POS);
int type   = OrderType();
bool result = false;
if(OrderType()==OP_SELL && OrderSymbol()==Symbol() && OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber)
OrderClose( OrderTicket(), OrderLots(), MarketInfo(OrderSymbol(), MODE_ASK), Slippage, Red );
else if(OrderType()==OP_BUY && OrderSymbol()==Symbol() && OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber)
OrderClose( OrderTicket(), OrderLots(), MarketInfo(OrderSymbol(), MODE_BID), Slippage, Red );
}
ClosePendingOrders();
}
}

void CloseAllOrders()
{
int total = OrdersTotal(),i,type;
for(i=total-1;i>=0;i--)
{
OrderSelect(i, SELECT_BY_POS);
type   = OrderType();
bool result = false;
switch(type)
{
case OP_BUY       :
if(OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber)
OrderClose( OrderTicket(), OrderLots(), MarketInfo(OrderSymbol(), MODE_BID), Slippage, Red );
break;
case OP_SELL      :
if(OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber)
OrderClose( OrderTicket(), OrderLots(), MarketInfo(OrderSymbol(), MODE_ASK), Slippage, Red );
break;
}
}
total = OrdersTotal();
for(i=total-1;i>=0;i--)
{
OrderSelect(i, SELECT_BY_POS);
result = false;
if(OrderSymbol()==Symbol() && OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber){
type   = OrderType();
switch(type)
{
case OP_BUYLIMIT  : OrderDelete( OrderTicket() );break;
case OP_BUYSTOP   : OrderDelete( OrderTicket() );break;
case OP_SELLLIMIT : OrderDelete( OrderTicket() );break;
case OP_SELLSTOP  : OrderDelete( OrderTicket() );break;
}
}
}
}

void closeTrades(int signal){
int total = OrdersTotal();
if(total>0){
bool closeSell = signal>0;
bool closeBuy = signal<0;
for(int x=total-1;x>=0;x--)
{
OrderSelect(x, SELECT_BY_POS);
if(OrderSymbol()==Symbol() && OrderType()==OP_BUY && closeBuy &&OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber)
OrderClose( OrderTicket(), OrderLots(), MarketInfo(OrderSymbol(), MODE_BID), Slippage, Red );
else if(OrderSymbol()==Symbol() && OrderType()==OP_SELL && closeSell &&OrderMagicNumber()==MagicNumber)
OrderClose( OrderTicket(), OrderLots(), MarketInfo(OrderSymbol(), MODE_ASK), Slippage, Red );
}
}
}

--- 帖子 #30 ---
Thanks for the questions mate. I appreciate for your interest.

The signal is based on 3 Indis such as Aligator with 2 EMA(5,10) crossing, Zigzag and RSI.

If each indi is bullish or bearish or non at all it will produce either 1 or -1 or 0

I summed all the result hence something like below

if it >0 then it's bullsiih (1,1,1 = 3)

<0 then it's bearish (-1,-1,-1 = -3)

==0 then it's neutral (1,0,-1 = 0)

It's simple, nothing fancy but it works ok.

Regarding trading using the line option in the backtest, I have not tried that yet.

But if it doesn't work, you can forward test it on a demo account.

--- 帖子 #32 ---
Yes when you set maxgrid to 10, it will open 10 order for each limit and stop orders, total = 20 and 1 opposite trade. Yes that's what I wanted, 1 losing trade covered with a whole lot of winning trading position.

In order to win with this EA, first you have to identify a trend continuation. Usually in a trend continuation you are in a range market in a short period of time. Let say you're in a bullish trend continuation and place the buy grid manually. Over that range market, it will trigger several buy limit orders and when it's going up, the losing position (sell) will be covered and triggered the buy stop order, hence you got 1 losing position + many many wining opened buy positions. So yes, they key success is identifying a trend continuation (range market that is not a reversal but instead a trend continuation). You can also win with this EA in a range market as well and breakout.

If it neutral, it won't place a grid, none.

Dynamic grid? My thought is, it's not a good idea because grid trading is meant to be fixed and better yet it's simpler. But do you have any reference for me to dive deeper on that subject, so maybe it could change my mind.

--- 帖子 #35 ---
In the EA properties or setting, you have to set the value of "How many stop/limit orders per grid" bigger than 0.

If you set to 0 then you will only open an opposite position trade without any stop/limit order thus no hedge. From the screenshot I shared, I accidentally set the value to 0 and maybe that caused the confusion.

So here's a better screenshot. Please note that this is just for an example sake

--- 帖子 #52 ---
TudorIoan...I am not sure I can see how this can be done?  As I see it, once you take trade 1, you can't move the entry point to #2.  And, if you take 3 trades at the lines indicated, I think we may have the following:

We're in a 1:1 Risk to Reward trade, where we seek 50 PIPS (in this instance).  In Example 1 (left), the trade is taken (#1), then price goes up, takes a second BUY, then a third BUY, and closes at +50PIPS.

Example 2 (middle), the trade is taken (#1), then price goes down and takes a second BUY (#2), then goes up and makes a third BUY, goes up further and gives +50PIPS total.  {Probably worth saying that each horizontal line is approx 17 PIPS}.  So, Trade #1 nets 34 PIPS.  It loses 17, then goes back up 51PIPS to net 34.  Trade #2 starts lower, and goes up netting +51 PIPS. Trade #3 goes up 17PIPS, netting 17PIPS.  So, total net PIPS for the trades would be:  34+51+17=102 PIPS.

Example 3 (right), the trade is taken (#1), price drops to the first line where Trade #2 (BUY) is taken.  Price drops further to the second line down where Trade #3 occurs, also a BUY.  Then, price goes up to the first line above the initial entry point and closes there.  My summation of the win is:  Trade #1 is up 17PIPS (based on the assumption in 2 above. Trade 2 drops 17 PIPS before rallying and capturing 34PIPS net.  Trade #3 (BUY), falls a slight bit, rises to the first line above the initial entry, and nets 51PIPS. Total PIPS for these 3 trades = 17+34+51=102 PIPS.

That's how I would understand the diagram.  And, this is what I was thinking, as I drew up my chart.

Thanks folks...good stuff...love the thinking process.

--- 帖子 #58 ---
TudorIoan/Yousername, If each number in each example were a trade, the trader would multiply his/her PIPS and income from a straight BUY to the Take Profit point.  That's the value I see in Grid Trading.  If you pick the right direction, but the trade goes against you for a (manageable) while, you will earn more than if it just went directly to your target (Take Profit) point. And, you can use smaller lot sizes because you buy/sell in at multiple levels.

Good luck!

Derek

--- 帖子 #67 ---
This is tricky and full of negative assumption about the broker . I my self will start a brokerage business with my colleague. lol

Stealth mode to me is a good way to place a mega grid. 1000 orders.

But for getting away from volatility in the market especially in a high impact news, maybe not.

Several problem with that

1. we could have a duplicated order.

2. The grid space between some order could be offset by 1 or 3 pips or more

3. Unknown.

Issue 1 and 2 could happened because of high volatility.

For instance let say the stealth order started at 1.3333 and the grid space is 5 pips.

Then a sudden volatility makes the price went up 50 pips in a second.

All of your new order could be executed between 1.3350 to 1.3383. Because of that the grid is not evenly spread orders and causing imbalance in the grid.

Whereas using a built in order, the market will place the order exactly at the requested price so we can have a evenly spread orders.

Anyhow I will see what I can do. Finger crossed.

teeth_val=iAlligator(Symbol(),tradingTF,13,8,8,5,5,3,MODE_SMMA,PRICE_MEDIAN,MODE_GATORTEETH,pos-5);
lips_val=iAlligator(Symbol(),tradingTF,13,8,8,5,5,3,MODE_SMMA,PRICE_MEDIAN,MODE_GATORLIPS,pos-3);

MA setting
Inserted Code       fasterEMAnow = iMA(Symbol(),tradingTF, FasterEMA, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, pos);
slowerEMAnow = iMA(Symbol(),tradingTF, SlowerEMA, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, pos);

ZigZag
Inserted Code iCustom(Symbol(), tradingTF, "ZigZag", zperiod,5,3,0, i);

RSI
Inserted Code iRSI(Symbol(),tradingTF,14,PRICE_CLOSE,0);

TF is set to DAILY (fixed).

Alligator - default

--- 帖子 #77 ---
I combined Ali and EMAs into 1 method. That's why we have 3 instead 4, just to keep it simple.

Maybe you can understand this

Inserted Code       if ((fasterEMAnow > slowerEMAnow)
&& jaw_val<teeth_val && teeth_val<lips_val) {
return 1;
}
else if ((fasterEMAnow < slowerEMAnow)
&& jaw_val>teeth_val && teeth_val>lips_val){
return -1;
}
return 0;

RSI method
Inserted Code    double rsi = iRSI(Symbol(),tradingTF,14,PRICE_CLOSE,0);
if(rsi>65)//oversold
return -1;
else if(rsi<35)//overbought
return 1;
else if(rsi>50)//bullish
return 1;
else if(rsi<50)//bearish
return -1;
return  0;

ZigZag methods
Inserted Code int getZigZagPosition(int index){
int i = 0;
int zigzag = 0;
int zigzagIndex=0;
while(i<Bars && zigzagIndex<index)
{
double zz1=iCustom(Symbol(), tradingTF, "ZigZag", zperiod,5,3,0, i);
if (zz1>0) {
zigzagIndex++;
}
i++;
}
return i-1;
}
int zigzag(){
int i = getZigZagPosition(zindex);
double z = iCustom(Symbol(), tradingTF, "ZigZag", zperiod,5,3,0, i);
double close = iClose(Symbol(),tradingTF,0);
if(z>close)
return -1;
else if(z<close)
return 1;

return 0;
}
Correction zperiod is set to 5,

Therefore zz indi set is 5,5,3

--- 帖子 #103 ---
You can use this EA on mutiple chart.

When the EA opened a grid on one chart, it won't open another grid on another chart.

WHY?

Because the limit/stop orders could already be used 100% on the first chart.

So on the second chart, there's no limit/stop order left for it. In short, no more bullet rounds until the grid on another chart is closed.

HEre is an example

You have EURUSD and USDCHF

You opened a grid on USDCHF and used all the available stop/limit orders on the MT4 platform for USDCHF. Let say the maximum order is 50.

As you have used all 50 orders for USDCHF, EURUSD will not be able open a grid until USDCHF Grid is closed

Furthermore I think there's no way to find out the maximum number of orders a broker can handle with MQL4. If it's possible, then we could have some order management. Unfortunately it's not possible for now. Let see if it will in the MT5

For reference read below
https://www.mql5.com/en/forum/155714#comment_3800403

A user said "Broker dependent, some 100, some 1000, some don't care. Ask the broker, put it in an external."

--- 帖子 #104 ---
I gotta take my word back...

I forgot that you can know the allowed limit orders

using

(int)AccountInfoInteger(ACCOUNT_LIMIT_ORDERS);
https://docs.mql4.com/constants/envi...t_info_integer

Inserted Code bool IsNewOrderAllowed()
{
//--- get the number of pending orders allowed on the account
int max_allowed_orders=(int)AccountInfoInteger(ACCOUNT_LIMIT_ORDERS);
//--- if there is no limitation, return true; you can send an order
if(max_allowed_orders==0) return(true);
//--- if we passed to this line, then there is a limitation; find out how many orders are already placed
int orders=OrdersTotal();
//--- return the result of comparing
return((orders+(maxGrid*2)+1)<max_allowed_orders);
}

--- 帖子 #150 ---
1. I was thinking the order of closing the pending and active orders.

First delete the active order.

Then for the pending order, it should delete from the center rather the top and bottom.

Because if it deletes the pending order from the top and the bottom, there's a chance the market could executes/touches the pending order in the center.

2. Having some issue when I use a grid that has 100 pending limit & stop orders in multiple chart.

Somehow there's a limit a broker can cater those orders. So there should be a way to check if there's any room (available order) left before placing a grid.

Recently I planned to opened 200 orders on 5 or 6 markets so total should be >1000 orders.

But then there's issue, it got stucked in a loop for retrying placing an order.

Because of that each market has uneven/imbalance grid. So yeah, that's a broker's problem that needs to be identify so we won't have a bad grid.

--- 帖子 #157 ---
Damn, new versions coming quick like a shot! Thanks much for your effort, yousername!

Just in case you're looking for more ideas:

Auto-Breakeven

Trading grid is always related to bigger drawdowns, mainly because of economic events. Thing is, most of these impacts are announced even before they come. There are dozens of economic calenders out there, as you know. IMHO, high impact events are death to any grid strategy. But here's the point: We will never be able to only trade when no high impacts are around (or upcoming). Some grids take more time so the most logical consequence is to be prepared.

Lets say i'm trading a bullish grid of USDCAD. Next high impact event is US Unemployment Claims with a obvious negative forecast (compared with previous), happening in 10 hours. In my manual trading, id make sure - about 4 hours before impact come -  to get a breakeven with my grid. 1 hour before the impact comes (and breakeven wasnt reached), i embrace the possibility of losing and decide if close the grid completely.

Saying that to the background; is there any way you might add a "Breakeven"-Button to the EA's visual interface? If clicked, the EA will close the whole grid once its breakeven and disable the EA (to prevent it from opening a new one).

Drawdown monitoring:

Is there any way to display the maximum drawdown of the current grid in term currency and PIPS?

--- 帖子 #158 ---
Hi yousername,

The grid is taking good shape. If you can bring clarity to your methods it will be an excellent manager for Risk Reward and Grid.

I would use it more for  money management than for trading martingale itself.

I would prefer to wait for the trade as per my plan rather than trading impulsively.

Direction is decided by me based upon my view of fundamentals and pairs behaviour. It is totally subjective and is not influenced by any indicator at all.

I divide my trading money in smaller lots and make deep pip pockets (contract values ofcourse are smaller) and trade only after knowing total risk in advance.

If you can set up RR magic lines (two thick shadows), which sets up One position at xxx pips distance from Market Price and another at xxx pips distance in the opposite side of the Market Price. I will manually drag them and see if Risk and Rewards match not only my targets of profit and risk but they tally with my strategy.

I print on chart the indicators of Murrey Math and one more of the following strategies which can print horizontal lines on the chart for medium term (1-3 weeks)

Support and Resistance (zone indicator)

Fibos + Harmonics (road_map)

Fractals (Fractals - adjustable price breakout)

Average Range (daily, weekly, monthly) - DWMranges

Murrey Maths (mostly extreme zones and middle Pivot zone) - MurreyMath-Timeframe rev.

Previous highs and lows (D-w-mn close line)

I aim for confluence.  I will by drag and drop method move about the RR magic lines and visualise the big picture and trade only when I strongly feel that it will achieve 1 risk and 2 reward results.

At the same time I will visualise where the lines for pullbacks should happen. I will also visualise where recovery is needed to lower breakeven or pile up profits.

And then draw those lines.

In short, I am opening a RR box and then setting up smaller webs of probable pullback or recovery and trading with calm. It is like I have laid my fishing net and waiting for the fish to be caught.

I insist only on taking trades which can generate me 1:2 RR so that at the end of the day even if I score 50% loss and 50% profit, I will still be making good profits. Like this.

Three buttons will bring brevity:  (a) Printing Lines (for hypothetical or virtual plotting) which will set up RR box and smaller zones of pullbacks, pyramiding and averaging (inverse pyramiding) (b) Executing Pending Orders selected from the lines after weighing RR and the pros and cons of strategy which imposes horizontal lines on the chart for making quick decisions and finally (c) Managing Manually - after trades have been activated

After the trades are done I use this indicator (Show Average Entry Price) to manage manually. The shadow shows me profit (positive number), breakeven (if it is closer to 0) and loss (negative number) which I need to know how to manually trade in order to bring down loss.I find on mql5 site this RR manager doing similar job. if you feel appropriate, please refine and absorb this in your EA.

Since you are open to ideas, I am sharing my hands-on experience with you. If you think they don't fit in with your plans, please ignore them.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Risk Reward Order Manager

Risk Reward Order Manager is an EA that will help you a lot in order to follow your money management plan.

You only need to set the parameters according with your money management strategy, and drag resistance, support and order levels. And push order button!

EA will do following operations taking of course care of current spreadCalculate risk reward ratio Check if that ratio is in accord with your settings If the operation is in a good risk reward ratio , EA will show you button for place order ELSE he will hide to you so you have to follow your rules He will know which kind of order to set (buy limit, buy stop, sell limit, sell stop) Show you how much (in money) you are going to risk and gain with that operation Show you lotsize calculate for that operation in order to follow your plan Show you how far in pip SL and TP are Draw a red rectangle from order level to SL (possible loss) Draw a green rectangle from order level to TP (possible profit) Draw a lime rectangle (optional, 1 to 1 R/R projection) Important! One to one operation is a bit greater than that. I mean, to be profitable in long term i set default 1 to 1 operation with reward/risk ratio 1,1 that is not an error!

More than this, EA will always show following information:Current spread Minimum lotsize for this pair Pips value in money for 1 lot operation of this pair Amount of money used by stop loss  in ALL open operation by this magic number (in money and in % of free margin)

How Does it work?

Once you set and drag in your strategical level the five horizontal lines drawn by EA on initialization (Strong resistance, medium resistance (dashed) , strong support , medium support (dashed) and yellow  dashed order level line).
EA will calculate possible operation you ll can place. He will figure strong resistance line and strong support line as target , so, in according with your level order positionwill show you only operations you ll can open to follow your money management rules (is a bit difficult to explain for that I invite you to see screen shot and video attached).
EA will show you the button to place standard operation (if those stick to money management) and will show you on chart through green (for profit) and red (for losses) rectangle Place buy limit ( if order level is below price and will set strong resistance as TP and Strong support as SL) Place buy stop ( if order level is above price and will set strong resistance as TP and Strong support as SL) Place sell limit ( if order level is above price, and will set strong resistance as SL and Strong support as TP) Place buy limit ( if order level is below price and will set strong resistance as SL and Strong support as TP) All those button will set a single order with full amount of lotsize calculate according with your settings.

If medium support or resistance are below or above of 1 to 1 risk reward projection EA will give you a choice to:place a full (mean with lotsize calculated by ea) standard operation  place a full (mean with lotsize calculated by ea) 1 to 1 risk reward operation place both operations with one click but with splitted amount of lotsize to follow better the rules You ll find input variables in screenshot and video!

This ea will work with pretty all value pairs plus  xauusd, xagusd , it will not work with a lot of other cfd like uk100, ger30 and so on!

https://c.mql5.com/31/55/risk-reward...creen-6823.png

Guys thanks for the input.

For now i'm gonna improve the RETRY order (its when there's issue placing order).

I will place an input 2 variables that you can set "Retry" and "Retry Time Out (ms)".

If you set Retry to 100 and Retry Time Out to 10ms, then it will retry 100x to place order where each retry has 10ms timeout.

So in worst case scenario it will takes 1000ms to complete the retry. And when the retry fail, it will send an email and alert like the following

EURUSD FAIL PLACING ORDER @1.1234 at 13:00 2017/13/7
ERROR CODE: 148
Fore more info about the error please visit https://book.mql4.com/appendix/errors

Yes, I do.

This EA (all the new versions starting from 1.6) enhance that concept.

Look for yourself my detailed exposure down in my attachement.

You can apply RR1:1 very easily now, with the advantage that you can afford now to stand and resisting few levels that market fights against you.

...reloading your chances for a happy result

edit: adjusted error, example now is TP/SL 60 pips (3 orders at 10 pips space for 30 pips swing = 60 pips)

Supplemental lecture :
To set an endless pyramid pendings grid, adding blindly pending orders it's a dangerous thing to do in my opinion. Of course you can close on BreakEven on the market's corrections (for BE, the correction must be >1/2from original swing, ...by courtesy of simnz trader post here above) but over that point, the losing positions aggregate outcome might consume drastically your margin, then emotions creep in and determine a trader (noob mostly) to close too early or too late... getting closer to a glorious account bust
You can be successful for weeks, months, years on pyramidal adding, but is very probable that one sunny day you'll find your margin in a critical situation.
That's why I am for the StopLoss.
Well, even brokers love the StopLoss, because your prolong agony between the full equity strat and the Margin Call, brings them more cash.
But the point is that I use SL for me, not for anyone else.
And is my advice for all of you, guys!
Thank you.

--- 帖子 #246 ---
I presume you used GRID STYLE 101

Here's a scheme of Gridstyle 101, BUY GRID

Buy Stop

Sell

Buy Limit

Sell is the center of the grid

Buy Stop and Buy Limit are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.

So the SELL is meant to be a losing position that got hedged by the Buy orders.

Grid Style 111 Buy

Buy Stop

Buy

Buy Limit

As you can see the center of the grid is buy. On top and bottom of it is similar to 101 Grid Style concept, hence there's no hedge or single losing opened order

GRID STYLE 110 Buy

Buy Stop

Buy

Sell Stop

Grid Style 110 could not >1 hedge position depending where the market is going. I could have 4 Sell and 5 Buy trade or many other possibilities

I hope you get what I mean. If you don't I can illustrate it in a MT4 chart.

--- 帖子 #256 ---
Function pips2Points()

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

//| pips2Points() @http://kolier.li |

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

double pips2Points(double pips)

{

double points;

if(Close[0]<10) {

points = pips*MathPow(10,Digits-4);

}

else if(Close[0]>10) {

points = pips*MathPow(10,Digits-2);

}

return(points);

}

User Input Parameters

extern double TakeProfit = 10; // In Pips. Take Profit, Change to 0 if you don't want to use.

extern double StopLoss = 10; // In Pips. Stop Loss, Change to 0 if you don't want to use.

Implementation

tp = pips2Points(TakeProfit)*Point;

sl = pips2Points(StopLoss)*Point;

int ticket = OrderSend(Symbol(), OP_BUY, 1, Ask, 3, Ask-sl, Ask+tp);

found the above on google (i know 0 about coding lol)

So the SELL is meant to be a losing position that got hedged by the Buy orders.

I believe I have resolved the digit issue with 4 digits broker when placing the grid.

Please exploit it and let me know if there's any issue.
Inserted Code double brokerDigitsIssue(double pips)
{
double points=0;
//4 ot 2 decimal currency/instrument pairs hence a 4 digit broker
if(MathMod(Digits,2)==0){
return pips/MathPow(10,Digits);
}
//5 or 3 decimal currency/instrument  pairs hence a 5 digit broker
else{
return NormalizeDouble((pips/MathPow(10,Digits))*10,Digits);
}  Attachment 4 //Old one, I just re upload a new one

--- 帖子 #274 ---
Do we have an auto BE function?

Here is the logic:

The example is for the both cases, Buy Grids and Sell Grids

And the example is for the both cases, Winning Grid and Loser Grid.

I showed them different targets (different swings) for a better illustration of the concept.

The example shows that it always exists a BE level, no matter if Buy Grids or Sell Grids, Winning Grids or Losing Grids...

The example shows that the BE level is always at 1/2 correction from the original swing.(mind the spread calculus deviation)

I guess the main purpose of a BE option (after the trading Grid is already started) is to offer the opportunity to abort the trend or that particular market bias if the player has no longer analytical and tactical reasons to belive in it and in the same time to have the chance to get a BE if he let that Grid alive.

Caution: if you let a losing Grid alive (uncontroled), it might consume hard your Margin before market will come back at that particular 1/2 correction of the original swing !

--- 帖子 #283 ---
LOL, sure you will be able to set the breakeven value to your own liking. You will be able to set it in the EA's properties.

Here's a layman logic of the Breakeven logic.

1. Grid opened

2. You clicked the breakeven button to green

3. The grid only has 1 opened position at start

4. Further down the line the market executed some of your pending orders.

5. when you have >=2 order gets executed + breakeven button is green = BREAKEVEN function starts working.

You will also be able to set the breakeven function will be run there are >=X active orders.

SO there will be 3 paratemers

Parameter 1) Use Breakeven? (Boolean)

Parameter 2) Breakeven amount (double amount $$$)

Parameter 3) Breakeven triggered after X opened orders (integer)

--- 帖子 #331 ---
After doing some investigation on the FLEXY GRID's setting reset to default whenever the MT4 rebooted or change template.

I found come to a conclusion.

Whenever you modify the value of the "EXTERN" variable when the program/EA is running, it won't be reflected into the EA Properties.

Please try this EA for your self and see what I mean.

Inserted Code //+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                                  test Sample.mq4 |
//|                   Copyright 2005-2014, MetaQuotes Software Corp. |
//|                                              http://www.mql4.com |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property copyright   "2005-2014, MetaQuotes Software Corp."
#property link        "http://www.mql4.com"
extern double test = 50;

int init(){
Alert("A ",test);
test=11;// simulate a button clicked.
Alert("B, ",test);
/*
go check the EA property.the Test input doesnt change from 50 to 11.
That is the issue with the button
*/
}

As seen in the example above we have 1 extern variable as input called "test". Its value is initialized with value 50.

Then when the init() method executed when the program run.

You will see a pop up message "A 50"

Lets pretend that button clicked and modify the test's value to 11.

It will show another pop message "B, 11".

Once you see those pop up messages, go and check the EA properties and see whether the test value changed from 50 to 11?

So that is the issue with the FlexyGrid's buttons. It will fall back to the default value everytime the template reload or MT4 got rebooted.

A solution is to set your fall back default value.

You can do so at the beginning when you first attached the EA into the chart. That is your only chance to modify the EA's property. Then when the EA is attached, you won't be able to modify the EA's property and you have to start over again. However you can still able change other properties such as the R:R value, lot size value etc on the fly. Once you have set the EA property, you may save it into a template and it will fallback to your default setting whenever you reload the template or reboot the MT4.

Regarding the "GRID STYLE" button, it will be fix in the version 1.9

Hi,

I worked on EAs for many years, most important things you need to keep in mind Specially with Grid Trading EAs:

1- Your Broker's Execution Slippage

2- Your Broker's Spreads

all EAs made good profit in the backtest from the big moves, and in big moves all Brokers make the spreads higher and you will have big slippage.

because that, there are millions of EAs work crazy in the backtest but on live account they dead.

Yes, once a price executes the Horizontal line, Flexy Grid removes COMMANDS (i.e. _2B) from the Horizontal's name. So that way when Flexy Grid touches that particular line again, it won't open another of the same grid twice,thrice,infinity

--- 帖子 #356 ---
From my experience ,spread is a big issue for all kind of grid trading . What usually happen, is spread sudden widen(occurs all the time, sometimes it's a deliberate action by broker) trigger pending stop order then reverse direction, very frustrating.

That's why a better approach is to use limit order instead of stop order. For buy order, EA monitors current Bid price, as soon as Bid price across above grid line (Ask price for sell order),place buy limit order at grid level, price will normally retrieve a bit trigger the limit order then continue go up. In a price rapid moving situation ,limit order probably won't be triggered, but hey, missing trade is always better than enter risky trade.

FLEXY GRID_1.9 (17 - 7 - 2017) #424
Updated as at 17-7-2017
AUTOMATED
SET A

Alligator - default

Zigzag, 5, 5, 3

RSI, 14

2 EMA (5 and 10) no shift
MANUAL

TRADING WITH LINES INFO:

Parameters:

Manual grid trading: True

Grid trade with horizontal line crossing: True
Example rename Lines:
NAME_1S

or

NAME_1B
1 indicates Grid Style 101

2 indicates Grid Style 111

3 indicates Grid Style 110

B indicates BUY Grid

S indicates SELL Grid.
HORIZONTAL LINE

NAME_TP

NAME_SL

NAME_C

TP = It will take profit (close the grid) when there's profit in the grid

SL = It will stop loss (close the grid) when the grid position is losing

C = It will close the grid
GRID STYLE (101 / 111 / 110)
Grid style 101, EG BUY GRID VISE VERSA FOR SELL

Sell Stop

Buy

Sell Limit

Buy is the center of the grid

Sell Stop and Sell Limit are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.

So the BUY is meant to be a losing position that got hedged by the Sell orders.
Grid Style 111 EG BUY GRID VISE VERSA FOR SELL

Buy Stop

Buy

Buy Limit

Buy is the center of the grid

Buy Stop and Buy Limit are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.
GRID STYLE 110 BUYS VISE VERSA FOR SELL

Buy Stop

Buy

Sell Stop

Buy is the center of the grid

Buy Stop and Sell Stop are the bulk orders above and below the center grid.
PIPS SETTING

5.0 = 5 pip for both (4 & 5 decimal accounts)
BREAKEVEN FUNCTION
BE (currency (&/or) pips) if BE true set 999999999 on the type not use by user
COMING SOON.
TRAILING STOP
FUTURE

AUTOMATION BRAINS (AI)
Send command/task lists to FG just like how you do it on SIRI/Virtual Assistance.
R&D
The custom grid parameter will be something like the follow
[10,5,1][10,10,5][10,20,20]

The example above there are 3 levels in the grid

first level has 10 orders, 5 pip distance, 1 lot per pending order.

2nd level has 10 orders, 10 pip distance, 5 lot per pending order

3rd level has 10 orders, 20 pip distance, 20 lot per pending order

You can have UNLIMITED until the broker dropped.
SIDE NOTE
YS - Your Spread
LS - Live Spread

possible issue with ordersend, slippage. In the code I converted the slippage input to 0.00xxx I just fixed it because it only accepts integer

i.e. 50 is correct. Not 0.00500 which was in the old code of version 1.9

Inserted Code int  OrderSend(
string   [i]symbol[/i][i],[/i]              // symbol
int      [i]cmd[/i][i], [/i]               // operation
double   [i]volume[/i][i],[/i]              // volume
double   [i]price[/i][i],[/i]               // price
int      [i]slippage[/i][i],[/i]            // slippage
double   [i]stoploss[/i][i], [/i]          // stop loss
double   [i]takeprofit[/i][i],[/i]          // take profit
string   [i]comment=NULL[/i][i],        [/i]// comment
int      [i]magic=0[/i][i], [/i]            // magic number
datetime [i]expiration=0[/i][i],[/i]// pending order expiration
color    [i]arrow_color=clrNONE[/i]// color
);

--- 帖子 #389 ---
yousername,

My suggestion on having compact interface. My suggestion for each module :

Screen Panel should have

Money Manage,

Plot,

Execute,

Order Manage

1. Money Manage:

Contract value to trade: 1k/10k/100k

Accounting Currency: US/EUR/Stg

Open Price: Market value

1 Pip value: (calculated by above three factors)

How much to trade: % of Equity (to calculate total pips that can be used and for lots)

Total No of pips to trade: xxxx (based on % of equity) or calculated manually and input.

Total quantity of lots that can be traded (based on total no of pips available)

Equity Risk Stop: XXX pips

The information will be printed as text on any selected corner of the screen.

Plot sets up hypothetical /virtual order lines, calculates risk/reward and allows drag and drop moving of lines to desired Pending Order placement.

Execute converts plotted lines into pending orders. Execute can be treated as a trigger Button for later stages as well to activate any embedded or indicator supplied strategy with its own Magic Number by adding an indicator trigger option.

Manage shows the progress of the trade , drawdown, trailing loss/profit, breakeven, facilitates adding or decreasing lots to manage drawdown and lower breakeven.

Ideal is by way of a moving shadow between Entry Average Price and Market Price. ALERT should trigger push notification on selection of pips drawdown, breakeven, proft/loss levels etc as desired by the user.

--- 帖子 #390 ---

--- 帖子 #391 ---
Plot (for news events or future planned days)

Direction: Up, Down, Both

Time-based: yes or no.

Both direction and timebased Yes selection will set up straddle (up and down) lines with different TP, and different SL for each direction and OCO (one cancels other order type). Time : start and end (2 SEPARATE INPUTS) : DD: HH: MM:SS. Trade expiry: XXX minutes after Start. tOTAL 3 INPUTS FOR TIMEBASED ORDER

Use Risk/Reward Lines (pips): Yes or No. Yes will show Market Price as default value and with an option to change the price level and open one line above market price/intended price and another below market price/intended price as per Risk in pips distance. Drag and Drop Lines to change Risk Reward will be ideal.

Do you want to set up straddle or individual trade or grid: Stradle or Invidividual selection will jump to set up lines.

Push Execute button ONLY when you want to convert the lines displayed into Pending Order.

Execute will convert lines into Pending orders with TP and SL.

--- 帖子 #392 ---
Plot (for directional trading)

direction: Up, down, Both

Time-based: No will show up Grid selection will ask for grid styles as per direction selected. Grid Style will be final selector. One grid style can be for UP direction, Second for Down and third one for BOTH directions.

If selected Both direction, Up and down grids should not have fixed TP and SL. Both should have flexibility with varying TP and SL inputs.

Not necessary to fill grid trades individually with TP and SL.

If selected both, Up direction can have grid of say 6 grids at a distance of 10 pips each with its own lots, TP and SL and at the same time Down direction can have

3 grids at a distance of 8 pips each with its own lots , TP and SL in the same single grid style.

Panel should be able to display all major inputs (excepting perhaps grid style inputs on pips distance, lot quantity, SL and TP etc) on the screen itself.

Alerts: proper planning of push mail/email alert messages will help save a lot of screen watching time. VERY VITAL IF MOBILE PHONE TRADING IS DESIRED.

--- 帖子 #426 ---
I just want to say

The trigger x pips/money amount will be triggered if the pips and amount you input is >0.

It will not be triggered if the pips and money that you input are a negative value

WHY? Because the point of Breakeven is to not make a winning grid become a losing grid when the market is moving not as expected.

For example if your GRID is in a green area, and the market suddenly go south, then the BE will save you from falling of the cliff.

--- 帖子 #431 ---
Good point. It wouldn't make too much sense to have BE triggerd based on X opened orders.

Break even is not depending on the number of orderes.

BE is the level always situated at half way of the grid, no matter how many orderes any particular grid has.

But I think it still be useful the have the possibility to call break even,... even on a losing grid.

Because a trader can hope that the price will turn in his favor doing a small correction  before hitting his SL(his maximum affordable risk), to a minimum recovery point, and that it would be the BE level situated at the half way of a negative losing grid

(refer to my drawings above on the thread)

As the BE doesn't have a trigger the BE is almost similar as TP

1.So when you open a trade and it has 1 pip profit.

2. Then you turned on the BE with 10 pip

3. When the grid goes from 1 to 10 pip profit, it will BE regardless how big your R:R ratio is.

As you can see, because there's no trigger on the BE, it acted as if it's like TP.

So here's the advise.

If you set BE to 30, you better turn it on after your grid has >BE+10 pips profit (in this case 40) just to be safe.

--- 帖子 #498 ---
If you are a programmer.

Your indi can actually open a grid with USE LINE.

Let say your indi says to buy.

When your indi gives a buy alert, it has to draw a HORIZONTAL LINE with name_2B or name_2S

Then you place the HORIZONTAL LINE at the market price.

If you want to close the order then draw the line and type name_C or name_TP or name_SL

--- 帖子 #499 ---
FG COMMAND is it calling a close grid indi as per pic ?

--- 帖子 #500 ---
Yes indeed.

Your indi has to draw a TEXT OBJECT with name FG_CLOSE.

FG will close accordingly and delete the FG_CLOSE command once grid has been closed

Alternatively as for now, you can use the HORIZONTAL_C at the market price in order to close the order.

If you place at the market price, there's a likelihood the market touches the HORIZONTAL_C

With FG Command, your indicator will be able manipulate FG's parameter.

You will also able to execute and close grid.

All you have to do is create a TEXT OBJECT and set the name with FG COMMAND

FG will executes all TEXT OBJECT that contains FG COMMAND and will delete the TEXT OBJECT after the command got executed.

--- 帖子 #514 ---
Let's presume you code your Indi.

When your indi produces a BUY signal and you want to execute a buy order.

Place a code as follow into your Indi buy signal function

Inserted Code ObjectCreate(0,"FG_GRID STYLE_111",OBJ_TEXT,0,0,0);
ObjectCreate(0,"FG_EXECUTE GRID_1",OBJ_TEXT,0,0,0);
FG_GRID STYLE_111 = Set Grid style to 111
FG_EXECUTE GRID_1 = Execute buy grid
FG_EXECUTE GRID_0 = Execute sell grid

Make sure you follow 2 steps above

1. Set the grid style using the Grid Style command

2. Execute the grid using the Execute Grid command

For more info about ObjectCreate
https://docs.mql4.com/objects/objectcreate

--- 帖子 #519 ---
For now FG is able to accept your COMMAND.

The USE LINES command

So let say you have a sell signal.

Your indi has to draw a horizontal line with name "YOUR HORIZONTAL NAME_2S"

If you want to set the TP, you have to draw a horizontal line with name "YOUR HORIZONTAL NAME_C"

_2S = Sell using Grid 111

_C = Close grid

So here's a code example
Inserted Code //Presuming you want to execute order immediately at the Ask price, do as follow
ObjectCreate(0,"YOUR HORIZONTAL NAME_2S",OBJ_HLINE,0,0,Ask);

//Close grid at price 1.1111
ObjectCreate(0,"YOUR HORIZONTAL NAME_C",OBJ_HLINE,0,0,1.1111);

Another example

If you want to place a pending order then you should change from Ask price to your own price. Let say the current price is 1.1234, your pending order is 1.1255
Inserted Code ObjectCreate(0,"YOUR HORIZONTAL NAME_2S",OBJ_HLINE,0,0,1.1255);
This mean the COMMAND _2S will be executed with it got touch.

--- 帖子 #522 ---
FYI, you can trade without having a grid.

If you don't want to trade with grid, you can set the GRID SIZE to 0 and set the GRID STYLE to either 111 or 110 because when using 110 Grid Style, the center of its grid is sell when you buy and buy when you sell. But for 111 and 110, the center of it is Buy when you place a buy grid, sell when you place a sell grid.

I hope you know what i mean.

Now consider the possibility with the FG COMMAND + your indicator.

You control the signal, trade and money management with command line.

There's no need to re-code complicated stuff like breakeven, trailling stop, R:R ratio, take profit etc.

All you have to do is setup FG parameters and place grid/order accordingly and through FG command only you can make it possible.

--- 帖子 #526 ---
Presuming the EA is already in the MT4.

Then you have to drag and drop the EA into the chart.

Then read through the input variables. I have made the input easier to understand for users.

==========

Since the update of the MT4 platform past build 600, there is now a new directory for installing your files. Previously you would simply need to install the file into the “experts” folder which is no longer the case.

1. To install your EA / Indicator, first please open your MT4 platform and select file in the top left hand corner.

2. You will then see an option to “Open Data Folder” – Please select this. Once this has been selected, the platform will direct you to a folder named MQL4.

The location may not be directly into the Metatrader 4 folder but a different location.

3. Please then open the MQL4 folder and paste your respective EA / Indicator files into their respective folders and re-load the platform.

--- 帖子 #540 ---
TBH I never use 110

I use 101 when i'm in the middle of a breakout.

For instance we just had an impulse move to the upside.

Market retrace 30%.

Some where in between retrace 30% I execute 101 grid.

When I execute that 101 grid at the 50% of the 30% retracement, it will pick up all the buy limit order and hedge the sell order.

Then surely it will go up and take all the buy stop.

That's the reason why I use 101.

However you must know that the market will continue it's momentum to the upside (bullish trend continuation).

If not then, you will have smaller loses than using grid 111. Because in grid 111 all orders are losers therefore bigger loser than 101 if the market continue go south.

Grid 111, I use it when a breakout about to start. Or during high impact news. It will execute all the buy stop order when the market spiked to the upside. vice versa.

--- 帖子 #553 ---
Here is TraillingStop (TS) logic

Let say the TS setup is the following

Trailling = 50

Trailling SL = 20

Let say the market went up 200 pips therefore it trails 4 times increase or 200/50 =4

0) Grid opened for the first time

Profit = 0pip

SL = No SL or will use the R:R Ratio SL

1)

Profit = 50pip

SL = 0pip (breakeven)

2)

Profit = 100pip

SL = 20 pip profit

3)

Profit =150pip

SL = 40 pip profit

4)

Profit = 200pip

SL = 60 pip profit

So when you are at the 200 pips profit and market turned sideway or reverse, your SL will stay fix at 60 pip profit.

Logic same applies to when you use TS based on currency amount

--- 帖子 #554 ---
Correction to the logic scenario

0) Grid opened for the first time

Profit = 0pip

SL = No SL or will use the R:R Ratio SL

1)

Profit = 50pip

SL = 20pip

2)

Profit = 100pip

SL = 40 pip profit

3)

Profit =150pip

SL = 60 pip profit

4)

Profit = 200pip

SL = 80 pip profit

80:200 is same as 20:50
R:R = 1:2.5

--- 帖子 #562 ---
I forgot to say that make sure the Trailling is higher the than Trailling SL

Here's an example when Trailling SL is higher than Trailling 40:20

0)

profit = 20 pip

sl = no sl

1)

profit = 20 pip

sl = 40 pip.

When you reached 20 pip, your grid will be closed because it's X=<40 (lest than or equal 40).

So make sure it's lower than the trailling or lower than 1

40:20 = 2 or 2:1 (WRONG)

20:40=0.5 or 1:2 (CORRECT)

Above are just an example.... You can set it to what ever you like as long as it is below than 1

--- 帖子 #599 ---
FG COMMAND update with the FG_CUSTOM LOT parameter

FG_CUSTOM LOT_X_0.01_3_2

X = increment style multiplication

0.01=your initial lot

3 = Incremented for each z order (in this case 3)

2 = Will be multiplied by 2

You can have either X or +

X = Multiplication

+ = Addition

Please watch, do miss it
Inserted Video

YOUR HORIZONTAL NAME_111_B

--- 帖子 #613 ---
I will give the latest build file update soon.

FG COMMAND LIST

1) BREAKEVEN

FG_BREAKEVEN_0/1_amount

or

FG_BREAKEVEN_0/1

i.e.

FG_BREAKEVEN_0 //Disable the breakeven feature

FG_BREAKEVEN_1//Enable the breakeven feature

FG_BREAKEVEN_1_5//This enables the breakeven and set the breakeven value to 5.

2) TRAILLINGSTOP

FG_TS_based(money/pips)_Trailling SL_Trailling (Reward)

or

FG_TRAILLINSTOP_based(money/pips)_Trailling SL_Trailling (Reward)

i.e.

FG_TS_PIPS_100_200 //This means for ever 200 pips profit, the Trailling Stop Loss will be increase by 100 pips

FG_TS_MONEY_100_200 //This means for ever 200 USD profit, the Trailling Stop Loss will be increase by 100 USD

This variable is independent to the R:R Ratio, so they are not related. Meaning if either one is triggered, it will be close.

Make sure you do not set the Trailling SL higher than Trailling value.

3) USE LINES

FG_USE LINES_0/1

i.e.

FG_USE LINES_0 //This disable USE LINES

0=disable

1=enable

4) BUY GRID

FG_SELL GRID

This is a command in order to place a buy grid

5) SELL GRID

FG_SELL GRID

This is a command in order to place a sell grid

6) CLOSE GRID

FG_CLOSE GRID

This command closes the grid

7) SPREAD

FG_SPREAD_your spread

FG_YS_your spread

i.e.

FG_SPREAD_5//FG will execute a grid if the spread is below your spread or YS

8) R:R RATIO

FG_RRR_rrBase(money/pips)_risk amount_reward amount

i.e.

FG_RRR_pips_500_1000//This means 500 SL and 1000 TP or 1:2 Risk Reward Ratio

9) BUY GRID STYLE

FG_BUY GRID STYLE_Alphanumeric(3 digit/alphabet)

i.e.

FG_BUY GRID STYLE_AAA //This will produces no sell grid

FG_BUY GRID STYLE_1A1 //This produces no order at the center of the grid but produces several BUY STOP and BUY LIMIT order

1=BUY

0=SELL

Alphabet=Non

>1=Invalid

10) SELL GRID STYLE

FG_SELL GRID STYLE_Alphanumeric(3 digit/alphabet)

i.e.

FG_SELL GRID STYLE_AAA //This will produces no grid

FG_SELL GRID STYLE_A11 //This produces no pending order at the top part but produces a SELL order and several SELL STOP order

1=SELL

0=BUY

Alphabet=Non

>1=Invalid

11) GRID SIZE

FG_GRID SIZE_total stop/limit pending order

i.e.

FG_GRID SIZE_5 //This will gives you 5 stop and 5 limit order hence total 10 pending orders

13) GRID SPACE

FG_GRID SPACE_pip distance

i.e.

FG_GRID SPACE_10 //Every order will have 10 pip distance

14) LOT SIZE

FG_LOT_lot amount

i.e.

FG_LOT_0.5 //This is static lot and apply same lot size across the grid pending order

15) CUSTOM LOT

FG_CUSTOM LOT_x or +_initial lot_orderIncrement_lot Increment

i.e.

FG_CUSTOM LOT_X_0.1_2_1.5 //This mean FG multiply the lot order size for ever 2 order by 150% or 1.5

Make sure the lot increment is bigger than 1 or else it's a shrinking lot size instead a lot size increase

15) RESET INPUT

FG_RESET //This reset all the input so that you can go to F7 (Expert Advisor Properties) in case you don't want to use the code for changing FG's properties

The command above are not case sensitive....

Here is an example of INDICATOR using FG COMMAND

I hope you get the point.... You can call FG_BUY GRID and FG_CLOSE GRID from your indi
Attached File(s)   FLEXY GRID_1.956.ex4

159 KB
|
363 downloads

Inserted Code int x=0;
int start()
{
if(x==0){
ObjectCreate(0,"FG_BREAKEVEN_1_123123",OBJ_TEXT,0,0,Ask,Ask);
ObjectCreate(0,"FG_LOT_2",OBJ_TEXT,0,0,Ask,Ask);
x++;
}
return(0);
}

From the code above the as you can see FG COMMAND is an interface that can be use and understand to HUMAN and COMPUTER.

--- 帖子 #623 ---
You need to use a FG Command if you want to change it.

FG_RRR_MONEY/PIPS_RISK_REWARD

for example

FG_RRR_MONEY_5000_10000 (1:2 RR Ratio in account currency)

or

FG_RRR_PIPS_500_100 (5:1 RR Ratio in pips)

FYI you can only change the EA Properties (F7) on the first time you attached the EA.

Alternatively you can also execute FG_RESET. Once you see the pop up, click F7, set your setting and click ok.

Fromm all I saying above there are 3 ways. Up to you which you want...

--- 帖子 #653 ---
I love using a trend line as a BUY/SELL signal.

Let say we have 2 Trend line forming a channel.

The top trend line is called TOP

the bottom trend line is called BOTTOM.

If both trend lines have a positive slope (ascending trend line) and the price is between the TOP and BOTTOM trend line then that mean it's bullish. FG will always place a BUY grid until it breaks below the BOTTOM trend line and it will stop placing a BUY grid.

I had this plan long before but never got implemented because I trade manually.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

--- 帖子 #654 ---

As for trend line I am using TL alert file attached.

--- 帖子 #655 ---
About this I will make a code to a HORIZONTAL LINE

NAME_grid style_B/S_PIPS_YYYY.MM.DD HH:MM_YYYY.MM.DD HH:MM

Grid style = 111 or any other combination
B/s = buy or sell
PIPS = triggered after X pips over the line
YYYY.MM.DD HH:MM = will be online after that particular time
YYYY.MM.DD HH:MM = expiration

--- 帖子 #674 ---
Probably I will do this instead

Horizontal name_execute multiple single order_n1_n2_pt1,ptn_sl1,sln

n1=buy/sell (b/s)
n2=how many orders
pt1...ptn=is the Profit Target. If n2 is set to 5 then there should be 5 PT
sl1...sln=iis the Stop loss target. If n2 is set to 5 then there hould be 5 SL

For example

Horizontal name_execute multiple single order_b_5_100,200,300,400,500_100,100,100,100,100

Command above will execute 5 Buy orders

with 5 TP starting from 100 ~500pips profit

SL all are set the same value to 100pips loss total is 500

--- 帖子 #679 ---
Successful traders really don't depend upon robots to think and trade for them.

EAs that plan to think and trade are good for video games. I have hardly found any auto trading profitable EA so far.

Semi-Auto EA is very effective. Auto EA is needed for executing trades.

Discretion should be used for bias determination, planning and mapping out lots and positions, and managing the drawdown after the trades are executed.

It will be quite useful (what you are attempting to achieve) is to have a script to place combination of pending orders, with unrelated up and down orders, with the ability to do:

1. place a pending order at Xx pips from current price or at a user set price level (entry).

2. an expiration of the pending order after X minutes

3. ability to alter some or all of the pending orders stop loss or TP levels in pips or price level.

The SL levels also need the functionality to be offset from each other by XX_pips so that SLs do not overlap at the same price level ... they must be all at different price levels offset by at least 5 to 10 pips or more but this offset value should be via user input so that a trader could input 5 or 15 or 15 or 20 or ..... 100 as the strategy requires.

Your EA will be a big big time saver when multiple trades are on the chart and your  script will make mundane tasks very simply instead of time consuming when changing all these settings manually in MT4/5 (which is rather annoying).

Wish you all the best.

--- 帖子 #680 ---
The future is not fully automatic but semi automatic where human and robot coexists and support one another.

Bright future for traders.

Fully automatic EA can't survive because the human including the institutional themselves hardly survive the market.

Any way with that said here is the latest version

1. Minimize and Expand the Info texts and calendar
2. FF Economic Calendar feature
3. NAME_grid style_B/S_PIPS_HH:MM

new horizontal code

i.e.

grid style = your grid tyle

B/ = B(buy), S(sell)

PIPS = A new trade will be opened XXX Pips after the lline got crossed

HH:MM= At that particular time the pending order is active and will opened the grid once it has reached the PIPS target.

For instance a horizontal price is placed at 0.8000

NAME_111_B_20_19:30

The grid that will be open is 111.

It will open a buy grid.

When the price crosses the horizontal at 19:30 it will place an order 20 pips when it crosses the Horizontal line.

Let say the market crossed to the upside that mean it will begin open the grid at 20PIPS + 0.8000 = 0.8020

If it crosses below then 0.8000-20 pips = 0.7980

--- 帖子 #696 ---
Here is the logic to the new line code.

You placed a code to the H line as the following

HORIZONTAL_111_B_5_10:00

1. Market crossed to the upside at >=10:00

2. FG Deletes the H line

3. Make a new H line +5 pips of the Horizontal line price with a new code such as "HORIZONTAL_111_B"

4. Set it invisible

5. Market executes HORIZONTAL_111_B accordingly when it crosses it.

--- 帖子 #702 ---
it's time to talk about entry and exit strategy because almost all feature have been implemented.

Here's how I take the trade in a trending market

1. Identify the trend. Presuming we are in an up trend

2. Look for the Economic calendar. If the expectation is lower than the previous result in an up trend market.

That mean the likelihood for positive news is higher...

3. Furthermore I look for a bullish engulfing candle where the wick is higher and lower than the previous candle. And the close is higher than the previous candle close/open.

4. Supporting point 3, it will be better if the volume has higher tick than the previous candle's volume.

5. Look for a buy position and use Grid style 111.

Working on the FG TASK command

Here's the plan

FG add task command

if the due date = 0 that mean execute now...

due date format

yyyy.mm.dd hh:mm

1. Create a horizontal line

FG_ADD TASK_due date and time_H LINE_your H line price_(Add the Horizontal codes that I shared last time)

2. Modify FG's parameter

FG_ADD TASK_due date_BREAKEVEN_0/1_size

FG_ADD TASK_due date_BUY GRID STYLE_style

FG_ADD TASK_due date_SELL GRID STYLE_style

FG_ADD TASK_due date_GRID SIZE_size

FG_ADD TASK_due date_GRID SPACE_pip space

FG_ADD TASK_due date_LOT_size

FG_ADD TASK_due date_RRR_money/pips_risk_reward

FG_ADD TASK_due date_TS_money/pips_risk_reward <--TraillingStop

you will be able to remove each task with a mouse click. I'll make a new info task sub window and place X next to each task.

--- 帖子 #717 ---
It is important to know the NEWS EXPECTATION and PREVIOUS RESULT.

If the trend is up and the expectation is lower than the previous result then that mean there's a possibility of divergence.

The news result will confirmed the divergence thus a reversal about to occurred. vice versa

If the trend is up and the expectation is lower than the previous result and the current result is higher than the expectation that mean we have a trend continuation. vice versa

If we are in a bullish correction (sideway, ABCDE pattern or any sideway move patterns) and the news expectation is higher than the previous result.

Then expect a breakout to the upside vice versa

If we are in a bullish correction (sideway, ABCDE pattern or any sideway move patterns) and the news expectation is lower than the previous result.

Then expect a breakout downward vice versa. However If the result is higher than the expectation, we should expect bullish trend continuation.

Basically it is very important to know what the expectation is in the context of the market trend....

Pay attention if the expectation is too optimistic or pessimistic.

--- 帖子 #718 ---
By too optimistic expectation I mean the market is in the uptrend but it's running out of steam...

And the economic expectation is higher than the previous result. That mean people are too optimistic about the result.

It's like the tower of Babel. When people are too optimistic and the tower gets too high (people gets tired to go up the tower carrying brick and mortar) then the tower will fall.

Pessimistic expectation is similar as above except it's in a downtrend and the result is lower than the previous result. However the result is higher than expected which lead to bullish reversal

--- 帖子 #725 ---
My trading was purely discretionary and based on having deep pip pockets (not necessarily deep dollar pockets) and working only on high daily range yielding pair of GBPJPY only.

The strategy is composed of two parts since I was not trading with stop loss.

First part was to jump into acceleration train for quick 15-20 pip journey.

Second part was risk management which required dependence on deep pip pockets to average adverse trades at every 200 pips movement .

Because of my vast experience in neutral (not directional) currency futures options trading, I will always go back to four months to find out the period's low and high

and plan risk management based on the distance between them. I will ensure +10% of the total distance is used  as equity loss stop. I will use lots and contract value as per the total dollar equity at risk.

I have given up this kind of trading as I have developed neck and back pain.

The first part required watching intensively just one pair GBPJPY for short-term acceleration of momentum (up or down) during Asian Hours by watching a matrix of eight mini-charts (subsequently mini Linear charts) in sub-windows as per this picture. https://www.forexfactory.com/showthr...95#post9585095.

I had done research first by building database of the size of the acceleration and probable times happening through an indicator. This gave me an idea that to earn 20 pips in quick burst will not be that difficult.

Initially, I started with having a minimum of four pairs moving in same direction and then jumping into the train. 90% of the time the trades were successful.

Subsequently I developed a feel for the probable moves happening and used to jump into on the basis of even two pairs moving in same direction.

Once in a while for using two pairs for guessing momentum speed, a trade got into adverse position. I used averaging to handle it. Because of my obstinate attitude on not having SL,the consequent drawdown was putting pressure on the psyche but I did not lose even a single trade. To avoid this psychological pressure, I later stuck strictly only to minimum of 4 pairs working in same direction if I were to trade. The silver lining was I learned averaging and varying lots in managing risk as well as my psychology well. In this trade no consideration was given as to whether the market is trending, ranging or reversing.

This phase of trading was too good to be true but it did not help my health. I had to forget about it.

Later, I shifted to trading through Quantum which was based on reversal trading, martingales, and discretionary risk management. This requires EA for shooting of trades and testing of pairs which will be suitable for this kind of wild trading. Till this date I haven't found any reliable EA for quantum trading. It requires EA trading indiscriminately with the reining-in done by manual risk management including using martingales and averaging. This kind of focus on risk management also paid off for this kind of MT4 demo-trading with too good to be true returns. I am therefore keen to pursue this because I don't have to watch the screen intensly for entering into trades and just focus on managing drawdown.

I use CME futures (not retail MT4 brokers who act against the traders by widening spreads). A reliable broker has recently introduced CME currency futures on MT5 platform. So a robot of quantum trading will come handy for trading with this broker. I will go for Quantum trading any day if a reliable MT5 EA is found.

Now I am planning to use zone trading because I want to stick to the risk management methods I have practised considerably. This zone trading will require determination of direction bias and sourcing trades with high risk: reward return. It will need a lot of patience and undoubtedly a fishnet has to be designed. Esimtate of trade duration will be another component which will help remaining true to strategy until the last minute. If you can somehow put trade duration vertical lines drawn as part of FG then your EA becomes my only tool for zonal trading in combination with your Zigcharm indicator helping me in determining zones.

--- 帖子 #758 ---
So here's the logic of the NEWS feature

It retrieves FF Calendar XML file once a week and parse it accordingly.

It doesn't have the ACTUAL data.
http://www.forexfactory.com/ff_calendar_thisweek.xml

Java come to the rescue to retrieve the ACTUAL data by web crawling FF's calendar website.

I programmed the web crawler to retrieve the data that I want and write it into a file.

Then FG merged the FF XML with the file that contains the ACTUAL data and display it to the screen accordingly.

Let's hope FF doesn't modify or redesign their website layout because if so, I have to re-programme the web crawler.

I presume you talk about GRID STYLE?

When you buy grid

1 = buy

0 = sell

When you sell grid

1= sell

0 = buy grid

That mean when you buy grid using grid style 111

Buy stop | Buy | Buy Limit

When you sell it becomes

Sell Limit | Sell | Sell Stop

If I'm not mistaken I think for Automatic mode I have not updated the grid style code.... So you will stick with 1 grid style 101.

Since EA will be producing signals (alerts) by push /email notification on the basis of seconds TF without requiring any bar construction or TF visualisation MT5 will be ideal.

--- 帖子 #783 ---
Sorry I misread your message. You have to click the row result and it should lead you to the latest result when you click it.

Perhaps try this latest update of the same version...

Regarding the latest update, you don't need to run the script again.

FG will run it automatically.

Why? Because Windows will close the JAR file in certain length of time of its run time.

In the latest FG, it will run the .jar file when the file last update age is>1 minute age.

For instance whenever Windows ends the JAR which lead to the file not getting updated for certain length of time. FG will check how long has the file not yet been updated. If it has not yet been updated for more than 1 minute, FG will run the JAR again and again until you exit the MT4 or end the FG

--- 帖子 #791 ---
it didn't happened to me........... ?

Now I updated the code to update every 5 minute

Inserted Code void runJavaActualCalendarApp(){
string src_path = StringConcatenate(TerminalInfoString(TERMINAL_DATA_PATH),"\\MQL4\\Files\\");
string actualResult="actual_result.txt";
datetime fileModifed=(datetime)FileGetInteger(actualResult,FILE_MODIFY_DATE,false);
double tdf= (TimeLocal()-fileModifed)/60;

if(tdf>PERIOD_M5){
ShellExecuteW (NULL, "open", "cmd", "/C javaw -jar "+src_path+"java_economic_calendar.jar "+src_path, NULL, 5);
}
}
Inserted Video

P.S. I found no problem when using on update every 1m or 5m

--- 帖子 #793 ---
For your issue try read this solution here

https://stackoverflow.com/questions/...-file/32426647

4down vote  Just came across the same problem trying to make a bad USB...
I tried to run this command in admin cmd
java -jar c:\fw\ducky\duckencode.jar -I c:\fw\ducky\HelloWorld.txt -o c:\fw\ducky\inject.bin But got this error:
Error: unable to access jarfile c:\fw\ducky\duckencode.jar Solution
1st step
Right click the jarfile in question. Click properties. Click the unblock tab in bottom right corner. The file was blocked, because it was downloaded and not created on my PC.
2nd step
In the cmd I changed the directory to where the jar file is located.
cd C:\fw\ducky\ Then I typed dir and saw the file was named duckencode.jar.jar
So in cmd I changed the original command to reference the file with .jar.jar
java -jar c:\fw\ducky\duckencode.jar.jar -I c:\fw\ducky\HelloWorld.txt -o c:\fw\ducky\inject.bin That command executed without error messages and the inject.bin I was trying to create was now located in the directory.
Hope this helps.

--- 帖子 #803 ---
The indicator is a mini chart with candles.

My strategy is to catch volatility spike in M1 timeframe for trading 15 m trend trending with a small pip target for a high daily range pair like GBPJPY.

I would load on GBPJPY chart, 8 times the indicator -each for different symbol to catch the momentum volatility.

For GBPJPY main chart, I would download the indy 8 times each with different symbols connected with GBP - GBPUSD, GBPEUR (mirrored), GBPAUD, GBPNZD, GBPCAD, GBPCHF, USDJPY, EURJPY and make it a matrix to detect alignment of atleast four symbols prices moving in same direction. This is purely price action.

I have loaded 8 indicators and made a matrix just for visualization for me to manually detect signal - xxxx pair symbols moving in same direction.

This kind of visualization is not needed for EA to produce signal.

The signal is produced by comparing direction of prices moving in M1 timeframe on chosen symbols The input for choosing symbols should be provided. If four or more symbols are confirmed moving in same direction (say Buy/sell) then EA set up on GBPJPY chart should set up buy/sell grid with TP of 15 or xxx pips and SL of xxx pips.

Filters should not be provided except for controlling frequency of signals.

If you can compare prices moving in seconds timeframe, (which I am told MT5 can facilitate) it will be excellent.

--- 帖子 #818 ---
There was a known problem when using FG in the MT4.

Whenever you click a button in the chart, it doesn't reflect the changes to the Expert property.

This issue has been posted in this thread. You have to look for it.

Because of that whenever you restart the MT4/change template, the property will revert back to default.

FG command solved that, it has its own way to remember the settings or in other word it has autosave feature.

So when ever to change setting, FG will autosave it immediately. That mean you don't have to worry losing your EA setting when your VPS/PC got rebooted or shutdown. This is a common issue to many EAs. It lost its setting when the VPS got rebooted.

--- 帖子 #919 ---
I use grid style buy: X11 and sell 11X. So I have 1 market order then the rest as limit orders.

I would like a higher take profit (profit target) for the 1st trade (the market order). So if the trade goes my way, I'll end up with the expected profit.

If in case the trade goes against me, it will open up more limit orders, and I would want to get out of the trade as soon as it's in profit, so a combined profit target for all open trades (which is the way it works now).

The only add on I'll like, is to be able to set a separate profit target for only the 1st market order. Then have the usual combined profit target in case the trade goes and opens up more limit orders.

Hope I explained it better. If not, let me know, and I'll see if I can draw it

--- 帖子 #926 ---
The key to an extremely successful grid is to incorporate individual stop losses and take profits for each grid level.

That being said, if you haven't coded that, this works quite well.

Made a 50% return in July (50k account). This grid has a 22% stop loss built in.

Interesting thread. Grids are aggressive so if you are going to try and run t hem, dont run them with a "minimalist" or "conservative" strategy.

Push them to the limit because if you catch the wrong side of the trend you will blow out anyway, doesnt matter how small your orders are.

You need manual intervention. For example, I didnt have the GRID in buy mode last week. That top at 1.19 was obvious.

I put it in sell mode. Now its back in buy mode, because we probably aren't dropping too much further (EURUSD).

TP is always 21 pips (from cost basis).

Also when your grid gets deep into drawdown, use your manual trading skills to snipe a high lot entry with a tight stop loss. You can recover that drawdown easier.

I personally run grids on as many uncorrelated pairs as I can.

--- 帖子 #929 ---
When you execute that command. That particular opened order won't be included into the take profit (groups) calculation.

If you want to include it again, simply remove the take profit level of the chart

--- 帖子 #930 ---
I have been following this way of trading for GBPJPY with no loss for last 2 years. I m bound to lose at equity stop loss  if multi year adjustments happen. Luckily I did no trade during Brexit because brokers increased margin money.

Presently It works well and generates up to 40% to 60% a month of return on margin money.

The skills required are:

*Ability to have deep pip pockets (15 times of daily range pips)

*Primary Bias determination on fundamental and technical factors based on discretion.

*Exercise patience to enter trades only when minimum reward is 2. 0 times of risk of 1. On GBPJPY when I entered sell at 146. 50 I determined risk at 200 pips aiming for TP of 400+ pips.

The concept is to be a nett winner.

If I lose 50% of time in 10 trades I lose 5*200

= 1000 pips. IF I win 50%*of time in 10 trades I win 5*400 = 2000 pips. Net winner by 1000 pips. U can spot at least one trade a month of this nature. This is in addition to grid trading. Patience is vital for this trade spotting method.

*Quick judgement to trade high lots with tight stop loss  as per your suggestion to recover from drawdown stage.

*Good EA to produce  combination grid with the ability to take profit and set stop losses for different grids individually as suggested by you (which I do manually but EA can do far better job).

*Ability to estimate probable time duration of the trade. It helps in sticking to trade setup patiently.

--- 帖子 #931 ---
New Un-Tested Feature except 2,3,4 and 6

1. News email alert X minute before released. You can set it to true from the EA Properties.

2. FG_SEARCH.

FG_SEARCH_anything you want.

This will perform Google Search.

This is convenient when you want to search for something like anything relate to forex or anyhing you want

3.FG_CALCULATE

This will calculate your input

e.g.

FG_CALCULATE_(1.0943*1.618)-1.618*2.5

4. FG_URL

This will visit a url

e.g.

FG_URL_FACEBOOK.COM

it will open a Facbook page

5. FG_NEWS TRIGGER

This will open a grid when the condition has met

e.g.

FG_NEWS TRIGGER_111_SELL_USD_GDP_ACTUAL_>_PREVIOUS

Command above will open a sell grid style 111 when the USD GDP Actual data is bigger than the previous

6. Now FG doesn't rely the FOREXFACTORY XML file.

It extract all the FF ECOMONIC CALENDAR directly from their page.

You must download JEC v1.zip file and extract the content into MQL4>FILES.

--- 帖子 #932 ---
Example of news email alert x minute before the news released

If you want to enable it, you have to go to the EA properties, scroll down and  set "Send email about up coming news" to true and don't forget to set the value after it to something else i.e. 5. If you set it to 5, it means 5 minutes before the news released, you will be notify.
