--- 帖子 #935 ---
I will make 2 new command

FG_LS/LOUISETANO_on/off(0/1)_100(TP in pips)

That mean it will be in Louisetano mode where the initial trade will have TP 100.

i.e.

FG_LOUISETANO_1_50

This will make the first opened order to have a TP target.

If you want to make check if the LS mode is on simply run the following command

FG_LS STATUS/LOUISETANO_STATUS
ie.

FG_LOUISETANO STATUS

This command gives an alert about LS status

Louisetano is on, 50

The trading manager feature in FG will close the trade if the first opened order reaches the TP i.e. 50 pips profit.

But if the market touches/opened the other pending orders, FG will cancel out the 50 pips profit target for the first order. Instead it will use the group profit target calculation i.e. using RR Ratio or Profit Target as group profit target calculation.

However when you click the close button. It will close out all the orders without considering the LOUISETANO option. Basically it will override and close the order in case of an emergency.

--- 帖子 #949 ---
One more additional detail...

If the pending order got triggered.

The Louisetano profit target will be multiplied by -1 therefore the value will be -X.

If you set the LS value to 50, therefore it will become -50 when the other pending order got triggered.

This will cause LS to be disabled.

It will be return back to normal non negative value when the combined profit target is reached.

200 = is the REWARD that you are eyeing for

that mean it is 1:2 Risk Reward Ratio

RRR = RISK REWARD RATIO

--- 帖子 #1020 ---
New major update to the Trailing Stop

FG_TRAILINGSTOP_PIPS_X_Y

X = Trigger

Y = Stop Loss

The new stop loss will be incremented for every pip increase in the profit..

0.Presuming you executed the following command

FG_TRAILINGSTOP_PIPS_30_10

Let say you buy EURUSD at 1.12000

new SL formula = P/L - X + Y

P/L = Profit or Loss

1. Later the EURUSD become 1.12300 (you have 30 pips profit and still floating)

New SL = 30 pips profit - 30 pips trigger + 10 pips SL = 10 pips at 1.1210

2. Followed with price increase again to 1.11245 (45 pips profit)

The new SL is 45-30+10= 25 pips SL which is at 1.1225

3. Followed with price increase again to 1.11260 (60 pips profit)

The new SL is 60-30+10= 40 pips SL which is at 1.1240

Right now the price has moved 60 pips profit and the SL has trailed to 1.12400 or 40 pips profit from 1.12000

4. If the price moved down to 1.12450, the SL will stay the same at 40pips profit

--- 帖子 #1044 ---
Thank you for the long questions. I appreciate that

1. 5 means, the grid will be close when the profit is equal to $X amount. In this case the X amount is $5

2. Logic is in post 1022

3. YS = your spread, or your spread threshold. If the spread jumped >5 pips, FG won't place a grid

4. LS = Live Spread of the market

5. FG_RRR_pips_39_22 that mean RISK:RATIO is 39:22. You are willing to risk losing 39 pips to gain 22 pips. Basically, 39 is the SL, 22 is the TP

6. FG_BUY GRID STYLE_AAA this mean no trade will be placed.

FG_BUY GRID STYLE_101 means BUY STOP, SELL, BUY LIMIT

FG_SELL GRID STYLE_101 means SELL LIMIT, BUY, SELL STOP

101 (from left to right)

1=The Top part of the grid

0=The middle

A=The bottom
Inserted Video

7. FG_CALCULATE_(1.0943*1.618)-1.618*2.5 it is a calculator function
Inserted Video

8. FG_LS_1_15

That is a louisetano's trade management logic

Poast 921, go start reading from there

9. Use Lines button, it will open a grid when the price crossed over certain horizontal line that has a command in its name

10. It's in the command list.

Presuming your horizontal name is Horizontal 234234234

You want to buy with 111 grid style

therefore

Horizontal 234234234_111_B

11. You just save the template just as usual

--- 帖子 #1059 ---
In the latest update for FG_2

Now FG can receive custom signal.

For instance, when you apply ZigCharm into your chart and then you press CTRL+B.

You will see an object called BIAS_bla bla bla

Notice the object contains a value 1 or -1
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

As seen in the screenshot above there are 3 BIAS highlighted in blue that FG will use.

FG will sum all those signals

1+-1+-1 = -1

That mean whenever the outcome is below 0, the signal is Bearish vice versa for bullish scenario.

When the signal is 0, that equals to Neutral.

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

In the screenshot above notice the value I input into "Signal names (separated with dollar sign $)"

I input the Object Name that was shown on the first screenshot into FG separated with $ sign.

BIAS_MACD_medium$BIAS_CCI(20)$BIAS_KC(10,0,5)

Attached Image (click to enlarge)

When there's no signal provided, it was NEUTRAL.

After everything is set, you will notice the SIGNAL changed from NEUTRAL to BEARISH.

1+-1+-1 = -1 which is below 0 and that equates to BEARISH signal.

Now you can go use your Indi and provide a text object or any object into the MT4 chart with particular name and its value is either 1 or -1 or 0.

Then you plugin the object name into FG and FG will follow the signal accordingly.

--- 帖子 #1085 ---
Grid style

BUY

111 = Buy stop, Buy, Buy Limit

101 = Buy stop, Sell, Buy Limit

000 = Sell Limit, Sell, Sell Stop

Sell

111 = Sell Limit, Sell, Sell Stop

101 = Sell Limit, Buy, Sell Stop

000 = Buy Stop, Buy, Buy Limit

From above you should see a pattern.

For buy case, 1 = Buy, 0 = Sell

For sell  case, 1 = Sell, 0 = Buy

Also notice reading from left to right, it determines the position of the order. The left is the top side, the right is the bottom side and the number in the center is the center side of the grid.

I hope you guys can see the picture.

That mean if you have grid style 010 and you click sell, you will see Buy Stop (top side), Sell (center), Buy Limit (bottom side)

--- 帖子 #1094 ---
I have also update the FG_2.1.ex4 so that it can run backtest. The old version 2.1 will not be able to be backtested because the EA thinks the .jar file doesn't exists although it does. Anyhow you must use the latest version attached in this reply.

In the video below I show you how to make a custom signal.

I hope after watching this video, you can make your own custom signal.
Inserted Video

The code below is what I use in the video.

Ofcourse you can use your own indi and produce the signal into a text object as seen in the video.
Inserted Code //+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                                 customSignal.mq4 |
//|                        Copyright 2017, MetaQuotes Software Corp. |
//|                                             https://www.mql5.com |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property copyright "Copyright 2017, MetaQuotes Software Corp."
#property link      "https://www.mql5.com"
#property version   "1.00"
#property strict
#property indicator_chart_window
enum indiPeriod
{
M1=PERIOD_M1, //1 Minute
M5=PERIOD_M5, //5 Minute
M15=PERIOD_M15, //15 Minute
M30=PERIOD_M30,//30 Minute
H1=PERIOD_H1,//1 Hour
H4=PERIOD_H4,//4 Hour
D1=PERIOD_D1,//Daily
W1=PERIOD_W1,//Weekly
MN=PERIOD_M15//Monthly
};

//--- input parameters
input indiPeriod   timeFrame=D1;
input int period;
input int signalId;
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Custom indicator initialization function                         |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
int OnInit()
{
//--- indicator buffers mapping

//---
return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
}
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Custom indicator iteration function                              |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
int OnCalculate(const int rates_total,
const int prev_calculated,
const datetime &time[],
const double &open[],
const double &high[],
const double &low[],
const double &close[],
const long &tick_volume[],
const long &volume[],
const int &spread[])
{
//---
signal();

//--- return value of prev_calculated for next call
return(rates_total);
}
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void signal(){
/*
Bear signal = price below the lower band
Bull signal = price above the upper band
*/
double lowerBand = iBands(Symbol(),timeFrame,period,2,0,PRICE_CLOSE,MODE_LOWER,0);
double upperBand = iBands(Symbol(),timeFrame,period,2,0,PRICE_CLOSE,MODE_UPPER,0);
double closingPrice=iClose(Symbol(),timeFrame,0);

string name="custom signal_"+signalId;
if(closingPrice<lowerBand){
//Bearish
ObjectCreate(0,name,OBJ_TEXT,0,0,0);
ObjectSetText(name,"-1",0);
}
else if(closingPrice>upperBand){
//Bullish
ObjectCreate(0,name,OBJ_TEXT,0,0,0);
ObjectSetText(name,"1",0);
}
else{
//Neutral
ObjectCreate(0,name,OBJ_TEXT,0,0,0);
ObjectSetText(name,"0",0);
}
}

Hello guys, first sorry my english...

I'd like to know if someone could make a Script or EA to Open & Close: Open_BuyLimit and Open_SellLimit
on the fibonacci retracement levels Drawed Manually in the chart. The strategy it's
based on Scalping with fibonacci retracement, so to get few pips.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
The retracement levels used will be: 100.0%, 61.8%, 50.0%, 38.2% and 23.6%.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Fixed lot size
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Rules for Open & Close Open_BuyLimit (2 orders):

1º Order:
- Open_BuyLimit it's executed when the price touch the 50.0% level;
- and is Closed when the price touch the 38.2% or 23.6% level; (configurable in pips too)

* if this 1º order Close in Protit on the 38.2%, or 23.6% level, the 2º order in 61.8 level must be automatically desatived.

2º Order:
- Open_BuyLimit it's executed when the price touch the 61.8%;
- and is Closed when the price touch the 38.2% or 23.6% level; (configurable in pips too)

The Stop Loss for two orders it's the 100.0% level. (configurable in pips too)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Rules for Open & Close Open_SellLimit (2 orders):

1º Order:
- Open_SellLimit it's executed when the price touch the 50.0% level;
- and is Closed when the price touch the 38.2% or 23.6% level; (configurable in pips too)

* if this 1º order Close in Protit on the 38.2%, or 23.6% level, the 2º order in 61.8 level must be automatically desatived.

2º Order:
- Open_SellLimit it's executed when the price touch the 61.8%;
- and is Closed when the price touch the 38.2% or 23.6% level; (configurable in pips too)

The Stop Loss for two orders it's the 100.0% level. (configurable in pips too)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* The Open_BuyLimit and Open_SellLimit orders, don't be must executed more one time if the price touch
the 50.0% and 61.8 levels again.

* Once time the 50.0% and 61.8 levels are executed, they must turn inactive, until a new fibonacci
retracement be drawned manually.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If someone make this, I'll be Very Grateful!!!

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Exemple:
Open_BuyLimit

and
Open_SellLimit

--- 帖子 #1134 ---
Assuming you buy with style 111, all the order and trade will be buy.

with the same assumption as above, for style 101, the middle part of the grid will be a sell trade (opposite of buy), while the other pending order will be a buy pending order.

This goes same as sell.

1 = sell

0 = opposite of sell (buy)

000 SELL = buy stop, buy, buy limit

000 BUY = sell limit, sell, sell stop

101 SELL = sell limit, buy, sell stop

010 SELL = buy stop, sell, buy limit

010 BUY = sell limit, buy, sell stop

Hopefully you see a pattern here

1 buy = buy

0 buy = sell

1 sell = sell

0 sell = buy

(non numeric i.e. XYZABCDEF) = no trade

XX1 sell = no pending order, no order, sell stop

--- 帖子 #1189 ---
1. Open a long & short grid at the beginning of the week (Sunday).

2. EA will close out the winning grid when the profit target is reached (note: EA setup for each grid). Keep opening new grids when this happens.

3. Decide to close out grids at the end of the week if the net profit exceeds the losses or carry over grid trades to the next week if open losses exceeds closed profits.

4. Keep testing this way until account reaches 100% return or -30% loss of initial starting balance.

Note: It would be nice to have the EA automatically open a new grid when the profit target is reached. Can someone please modify the EA and add this as an input?

--- 帖子 #1217 ---
Set your connection in the Control Panel to 'Metered'.  This stops Windows from automatically downloading and installing updates.  You can then switch this off at the weekend and download and apply any updates that are outstanding at your convenience.

Attached File(s)   TCO FG.mq4

114 KB
|
1,589 downloads

Hi Guys,

I have been lurking here for awhile. I'm attaching my EA, if the thread owner doesn't mind. It trades the 111 strategy automatically. It is a simplified version.

The EA will open Buy Grid and Sell Grid on same chart, and track profit for each grid. If the BuyGrid reaches it's profit target, the BuyGrid will be closed and reopened. The SellGrid will remain along with any open sell trades and vice versa. The display in the upper right hand corner isn't as fancy, as yousername presented, but it will do the job. You can also set a day of the week and time to close all trades for the given pair. There is an EquityProtection feature. so if you put in 0.30 it will close all trades, if your equity is down 30%. I'm sure there is some clean up to be done, but here it is. My contribution. It seems to be working fine for me. I put it on 28 pairs on a $10,000 demo account just to wring it out and stress my CPU. If you are going to do something crazy like that. I would attach it to one chart and let it open all the trades first and then open the next chart and so on. I did that yesterday and it took awhile. I'm just running it on 28 charts for now to see how it works and find what pairs will be more successful. At the moment, I'm not sure if I will close all trades at the end of the week or not.

Here are the inputs:

CloseAllTrades = false; <== Emergency Close all trades for the pair

UseProfitGoal = true; <== Use Profit Goal for each Grid

ProfitGoal = 5.00; <== Profit Goal is $5.00, all trades will be close for grid that is in profit once goal is met.

BuyGrid = true; <== Allow BuyGrid to be opened

BuyMagicNumber = 11111; <== Must have BuyMagicNumber and it must be different from SellMagicNumber

SellGrid = true; <== Allow SellGrid to be opened

SellMagicNumber = 22222; <== Must have SellMagicNumber and it must be different from BuyMagicNumber

GridStep = 5; <== Distance between trades in pips

MaxOrders = 40; <== Number of total Limit/Stop orders, so for 40, 20 Limit 20 Stop orders and 1 market order for 41 total, 41 for

BuyGrid and 41 for SellGrid, total of 82 per pair, if you use 40, if you put 20 it would 42 total orders.

LotSize = 0.01;

CloseAllTradesDayTime = true; <== Close trades on a certain day after a certain time

CloseWeekday = 5; <== 1-Monday, 2-Tuesday, 3-Wednesday, 4-Thursday, 5-Friday

CloseHours = 22; <== Close Hour

CloseMinutes = 30; <== Close Minutes

UseEquityProtection = true; <== Use Equity Protection

EquityProtectionPercent = 0.30; <== Close all trades if equity drops 30%

--- 帖子 #1337 ---
iTime() returns a datetime value
Attached Image (click to enlarge)

You'll have to typeCast the value returned to your desired type.

Am not sure whether time_bal is a double or an int in your code.

If it's an int edit the code this way:
Inserted Code time_Bal = (int)iTime(Symbol(),BreakTime,0)

if it's a double:
Inserted Code time_Bal = (double)iTime(Symbol(),BreakTime,0)

You can also change time_Bal to a datetime type and also go through the code and make sure changing it to datetime doesn't affect the math/algorithm in the code.

--- 帖子 #1346 ---
Thats very good to hear Richard!!

I have been using grid eas till now and like it alot, but sometimes it can be to high dd. And I think my new idea can be very profitable. To reduce the dd if the trend is getting stronger.

So my idea is:

1. Buy (0.01 lot ) and 1 sell (0.01 lot ) is open at same time (tp is adjustable)

2. Next trade open (sell goes in profit and open a new one right away with same lot (0.01) and buy (0.02 lot ) open another one. That will be 2nd level)

3. Next trade open (sell goes in profit and open a new one right away with same lot (0.01) and buy (0.03 lot) open another one. That will be 3rd level)

4. Next trade open (sell goes in profit and open a new one right away with same lot (0.01) and buy (0.04 lot) open another one. That will be 4th level)

5. Next trade open (sell goes in profit. And now here is the part i think we can reduce the DD. It open sell with higher lot let say 0.03 (adjustable) Buy open with 0.05. 5th level)

6. Next trade open (sell open a new trade with 0.04 lot and buy with 0.06)

And this will continue till the trend goes opposite direction. So now we have 6 buy and 2 sell. The trend is going up(no more trades is executed, we will only focus to get this trades in profit ) and all trades is going in profit and now we have some profit (here we can have the option to adjust the amount ) trades is in tp and closed.

7. We start from the beginning

If you can code this ea i will be very grateful!

Best regards

Henning
